\\n149: ## Remote storage integrations\\n150: \\n151: Prometheus's local storage is limited to a single node's scalability and durability.\\n152: Instead of trying to solve clustered storage in Prometheus itself, Prometheus offers\\n153: a set of interfaces that allow integrating with remote storage systems.\\n154: \\n155: \",\"endLine\":155,\"startLine\":148},{\"content\":\"172: \\n173: For read](configuration/configuration.md#remote_read) sections of the Prometheus\\n176: configuration documentation.\\n177: \",\"endLine\":177,\"startLine\":172},{\"content\":\"156: \\n157: Prometheus integrates with remote storage systems in four ways:\\n158: \\n159: - Prometheus can write samples that it ingests to a remote URL in a [Remote Write format](https://prometheus.io/docs/specs/remote_write_spec_2_0/).\\n160: - Prometheus can receive samples from other clients in a [Remote Write format](https://prometheus.io/docs/specs/remote_write_spec_2_0/).\\n161: - Prometheus can read (back) sample data from a remote URL in a [Remote Read format](https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/blob/main/prompb/remote.proto#L31).\\n162: - Prometheus can return sample data requested by clients in a [Remote Read format](https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/blob/main/prompb/remote.proto#L31).\\n163: \\n164: ![Remote read and write architecture](images/remote_integrations.png)\\n165: \\n166: The remote read \n149: ## Remote storage integrations\n150: \n151: Prometheus's local storage is limited to a single node's scalability and durability.\n152: Instead of trying to solve clustered storage in Prometheus itself, Prometheus offers\n153: a set of interfaces that allow integrating with remote storage systems.\n154: \n155: ","endLine":155,"startLine":148},{"content":"172: \n173: For details on configuring \n159: - Prometheus can write samples that it ingests to a remote URL in a [Remote Write format](https://prometheus.io/docs/specs/remote_write_spec_2_0/).\n160: - Prometheus can receive samples from other clients in a [Remote Write format](https://prometheus.io/docs/specs/remote_write_spec_2_0/).\n161: - Prometheus can read (back) sample data from a remote URL in a [Remote Read format](https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/blob/main/prompb/remote.proto#L31).\n162: - Prometheus can return sample data requested by clients in a [Remote Read format](https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/blob/main/prompb/remote.proto#L31).\n163: \n164: ![Remote read and write architecture](images/remote_integrations.png)\n165: \n166: The remote read and
